Comment Value: Sibusiso it was a pleasure to meet you and to assist in optimising your health. The last 2 years have been difficult - especially when it comes to routine and being able to stick to certain goals. Lifestyle change is essential.
It will help you maintain a healthy BMI, improve your blood pressure, decrease your cholesterol and insulin levels.
There is a dietician at the Wellness Centre if you need advice on how to achieve this through an adjusted diet. Be more active, spend more time with your loved ones, breath more!
We look forward to seeing you again.
